Huge underground garage convenient to Asian Art Museum, Brooks Hall, City Hall, Davies Symphony Hall, and Opera House. Space available posted on Franklin Street, entry on McAllister Street. <review>Don't get your car locked in 30 (whenever) minutes before its supposed to close. (I was sober and fully functioning)

Do not gamble with this garage past 9PM. It is not directly owned by the city and closes whenever the owner feels like closing. I arrived before 11:30 and had to be back in the city at 6AM to get my car. No fines or anything. But this is unreliable. Take your chances elsewhere, cheap though! But not worth it.

<Name>David W.<//Name><text>I parked here today, on a Thursday sunny morning (11:45am), March 26th, 2015.  First, I must inform everybody that this location is a safe-haven for many of the debilitated  homeless.  And you will see them loitering around next to trees, littering, smoking, and camping on the lawns.  Second, the staircases technically serve as their urinals; so be prepared to hold your breath, watch out for the puddles, and the buzzing flies; definitely a sanitary issue here!  Third, the elevators also have flies and littering, but without the smell, luckily that is.  Fourth, every level of the garage was packed beyond imaginable capacity, even at the above morning time-frame.  I was just lucky, because someone just happened to be pulling out.  So be prepared to circle around, until someone pulls out; a lot of patience here.  Fifth, and finally, the good news -- this parking garage implements a full security team.  The garage is monitored with digital PC surveillance, multiple patrol guards driving and walking around every level, and even a surface team scouting the entrances, staircases, and elevators.  Don't be surprised to see a lot a luxury cars parking here; I parked next to a new Porsche 911 GT, and across from several BMWs and Lexus.  Mostly likely due to the high level of security here.  But please note, everything that I observed was during the day time; so I don't know what the security staff is like during night hours.  And also, this review is strictly to inform future customers, based on what I have observed that day.  By no means it was meant to be offensive. < review>
I love this place so much. It is my go to Mexican restaurant. When I lived across the street I would frequent this place probably 4 times a week.
I come from Salinas where you get true authentic Mexican food and when I moved to the Sacramento area I couldn't find that anywhere till I visited this place.
Their food is fresh, and always has an amazing flavor.
The owners and workers are so friendly and kind. They gave me a shirt for free for going there so often.
And when my father got very sick, he couldn't eat anything. He didn't want to come here cause he never had an appetite. I watched him eat an entire plate and then order left overs. Now when he comes and visits from Salinas he always asks to go to el sombrero while we are here.
The Linares' s love you guys! It's like a little piece of a home away from home for me! Don't change a bit!</review>

100789076754185939604<//userid>
< text>
Summary: Quality is good, taste is good (but varies by item), value is excellent. The staff is friendly, but food production was slow when I went on a Thursday evening (one cook and three others).  The restaurant also had large flies flying around (including in the kitchen). Good, but not the best I've ever had.

I went here on a Thursday at around 7pm and there were two other people eating in the restaurant. In order to sample the wares, I decided to try a carne asada, carnitas, al pastor, and chicken soft taco. The total for the four came to about $9.60.  I then filled up my little bag with chips and took some salsas to go, and sat down to wait for my food to be ready.

There were two girls working the register and cleaning up/delivering food items, and one woman cooking the food (another non-cook appeared from the back later).  The cook was hard at work building a large to-go order, and it took about 15 minutes for me to get my four tacos. In the meantime, a couple of parties with kids arrived and placed their orders and sat down to eat at the restaurant. Unfortunately, flies were flying around and getting on myself and the other guests.

When my food was ready, I took it home and began eating. The chunky salsa was good, the tomatillo was my favorite, and the thinner red salsa was alright.  The carne asada and al pastor were my favorite. Tasty, nice textures, and good quality.  The al pastor had a slight sweetness from the marinade, which worked well. The carnitas and chicken were both very tender, but didn't have a lot of flavor, unfortunately. Still, for the price, it was a pretty good dinner and a solid value.< /text>

<userid>113868356901293728021</userid>< text>
The staff was tired after their dinner rush (understandable), they forgot to give us our drinks then forgot to give us extra stuff we paid for on the side. When the food arrived it wasn't as hot as other restaurants. Serving portions for the price were good.  I told them just cilantro & green mild sauce & all of the tacos had a spicy red sauce poured over them.  I tried to eat them but my mouth was burning. The surf & turf super burrito was extremely mushy like they blended everything then poured it into a burrito. The Spanish rice tasted like white rice. A couple of bites were so bland it made my stomach turn because it tasted the way wet paper towels smell. The asada fries came with a spoon & soon we seen why.  There was a  juice settled at the bottom that made the fries wet & soggy. It was like eating asada fries soup. We will NOT be back for hot food. We will be back to try dessert!<//text>

Saw this on the Stockton Savings Pass app and gave it a try just because it had a deal available. I fell in love with it since then. I also got my brother to love their carne asada fries. Their shrimp burritos are also a must try. Customer service is superb, it is family-owned and one can really witness the passion they put into the business. < Text>
A few days ago, I noticed that a portion of the front yard was soaked with water with some pudding near the house around our tree and shrubs.  I made sure that the sprinklers were not leaking and that left only one possible source of the water and that would have to be the main water supply to the house.  I called Advanced Plumbing by chance and that same day Jason came out to take a look.  He was very pleasant and helpful.  He turned the main water supply off at the house and checked the water meter near the street.  The meter showed that water was still passing at a rate of .2 of a cubic foot per minute.  Jason showed me and explained that it could only be a leak in the main water supply.  Jason then checked the water pressure at the garden hose spigot, it was a little low.  He told me that he could replace the main supply piping and would email me an estimate.  I called other plumber services and another company came out and without checking the meter or water pressure told me that I needed a new water supply line.  Another company used Google maps satellite view to look at my house and gave me a quote without even coming out to meet.

Jason emailed an estimate in a short time and called me to follow up if I had any questions.  The estimate was not the lowest however Jason was the only person to actually diagnose where the water was leaking.  Later that day I called Jason and we booked the job.  Jason told me that he would come out the next morning at 10:00.  He called before 10:00 to tell me he would be about an hour late.  Forty five minutes later Jason arrived and began work.  He replaced the leaking PVC plastic line that was 30 plus years old with a new copper line.  He was always friendly and answered all of my questions.  There was minimal intrusion in our lawn or landscape.  He and a helper completed the job in approximately four hours, turned our water back on and leak checked all connections.  I was very pleased with the service Jason and Advanced Plumbing provided.  I would recommend them to others.</Text>

My Story.....I‚Äôve lived in this area since 1975, I‚Äôve have had several different plumbing challenges, and used various companies. Now I am retired on a very fixed income.  I knew the work I needed done was extensive, lots of leaks, toilet faucets etc., a RO system had to be installed, a line needed to be run under the house for refrigerator water, and the water heater had an over flow issue, This was discovered when it flooded into the garage.  Come to find out the overflow from the water heater should have been routed outside, and wasn‚Äôt even to code.
I phoned a few plumbing companies about my issues and obtained several quotes. The job was time sensitive. The other item was a small dripping leak under the house he noticed, when he went under the house for the refrigerator line, this leak was coming from the shower area. <Review>Prior Employee 2013 - In the time I worked for this company I unfortunately walked away disappointed. I have over 25 years experience in the mortgage industry and I do not have one unkind word for any of my prior employers. In those years I received numerous service excellence awards, cards and letters of appreciation for the job I do as a professional. At Springboard, I learned that none of this mattered, there is a strong alliance between the Latino/Hispanic staff. And what I saw was a jealousy or what is better described as fear of an individuals personal growth within the company. I found myself definitely questioning their ethics and integrity here. The employee atmosphere is tense, stressful and unprofessional to say the least. The quality of service depends on the mood of management . They run this organization like a sweat shop/slave driven workshop, "numbers over quality." Absolutely no respect for employees. I would highly recommend going somewhere else for assistance as they do train new employees for 2 weeks only to place them on a floor of supervisors or "team leads" with no respect for managerial authority. Simple case of "Too many Chiefs, not enough Indians." Each Team Lead has his or her rules, and they want you to follow them and not management, which is confusing for a new person. Follow at your own risk, in my experience this type of managerial floor breeds back biting and dishonesty which will yield failure in the end. Overall, the training was great but was not reflected in service. Personally, I thought after attending training needed to be shortened and revamped according to employee or customer feedback.
